this.tick = function(game) {
  var mSize = this.options.map_size;
  var multiplier = 1875; 
  
  for (let ship of game.ships) {
    var vx = ship.vx || 0;
    var vy = ship.vy || 0;
    var speed = Math.sqrt(Math.pow(vx, 2) + Math.pow(vy, 2));
    var displaySpeed = Math.round(speed * multiplier);

    var textColor = "#DDDDDD"; 
    if (displaySpeed >= 1224) {
      textColor = "#F0C68C"; 
    }

    ship.setUIComponent({
      id: "speedometer",
      position: [-2, 28.5, 20, 5], 
      clickable: false,
      visible: true,
      components: [
        { 
          type: "text", 
          position: [-30, -8, 130, 130], 
          color: textColor, 
          value: displaySpeed + " km/h", 
          align: "right",
          font: "Courier" 
        }
      ]
    });
  }
  if (game.step % 60 === 0) {
    var aliens = Math.max(20,Math.min(2,game.ships.length*1));
    if (game.aliens.length<aliens)
    {
      var minute = game.step/3600 ;
      var range = Math.min(alien_types.length,minute/1);
      var index = Math.floor(Math.random()*range);
      var angle = Math.random()*Math.PI*2;
      var alien = alien_types[index] ;
      alien.x = Math.cos(angle)*350 ;
      alien.y = Math.sin(angle)*350 ;
      game.addAlien(alien) ;
    }
    for (var i=0;i<game.ships.length;i++)
    {
      var ship = game.ships[i];
      if (ship.custom.radar_updated === null)
      {
        ship.custom.radar_updated = true ;
        ship.setUIComponent(radar_background);
      }
    }
  }
};
this.event = function(event, game) {
  switch (event.name) {
    case "game_over":
      for (let ship of game.ships) {
        ship.setUIComponent({ id: "speedometer", visible: false });
      }
      break;
  }
};
